< Review>
I love Oceanside Dental Arts for a few reasons!

First and foremost, Diane!!! Best hygienist ever. She is thorough with a light touch and it feels more like a relaxing spa day than a dental cleaning. I also love chatting with her and catching up every six months. She is wonderful and I highly recommend her to anyone. My two sons had to join me for one cleaning (ages 6 and 7 at the time) and she was really awesome talking to them and including them in the conversation and making it fun instead of boring for them.

Secondly, Dr. Chang is great. He always stops by during my cleanings, checks everything out, is professional, explains things well, and also tells me what he is doing during the exam as he does it which I appreciate.

Finally, the office runs smoothly, and has great staff that enjoys it there. Appointments always feel like you get what you need and they spend the time with you needed, but also that they get you in and out relatively quickly. It's a fine balance but they have it down.

Oceanside Dental Arts is an upscale dental office that still feels friendly and homey. I always feel I'm in good hands, with honest assessments of my teeth, and no one trying to up-sale me on anything.< /Review>

<name>Joseph Sze</name>< date>
1519939841947<//date>
<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
The place is decorated very nicely, clean carpets throughout, which also keeps the area quiet.

Entertainment TVs everywhere, in front of both the main entrance and the examination seats. Could be even nicer of the tv is a bit higher there so it‚Äôs possible to see it while the chair is reclined.  In addition there is a monitor screen that can instantaneously display X-ray images and makes the office pretty much paperless.

The check in staff is pretty nice and I was seen by the equally friendly hygienist around my scheduled appointment time, who was pretty through with cleaning and polishing every corner. Best of all they offered me a pair of dark goggles to keep filter the light and keep splashing water out. Speaking of which the hygienists here usually only use a focused light rather than the large overhead light which further reduces glare. Dr. Stuart Chang also came in himself and explained in what ways my cleaning habits are good and what needs working on.

In conclusion Oceanside Dental Arts is a pretty modern looking and clean Dental clinic.It‚Äôs as modern as you can get with traditional dentistry around here.< /review>

I never thought I'd enjoy a boxing class, but I tried it out when I was feeling especially frustrated and was surprised by the whole-body workout I got. There are people of all body types and abilities, and you do whatever you are able to do. The instructors keep it fun, and there are segments (I think 3 minutes), so you can ease your way through the class a bit at a time. Great for exercise and for working out your frustrations - I can't wait until they can reopen!<//text>

I then came back the very next day early in the AM to tell them what had happened, and and got my appointment rescheduled for the next day.
After passing my written test, I made my behind the wheel drivers test for the very next day. I show up, go into inspection, and this elder lady named 'Olga B.' (mid 50s, 60s blonde) was demanding things from me while doing the inspection, like: "turn on the left blinker now!" After her demanding things, and me politely following her instructions, saying "Yes ma'am." after EVERYTHING she demanded, she gets in my vehicle, sees my tattoos, makes a disturbing sound and asked me if I was an "affiliate in any way."
